And a fire was kindled in their company; the flame burned up
the wicked.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

They made a calf in Horeb, and worshipped the molten image.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

Thus they changed their glory into the similitude of an ox that
eateth grass.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

They forgat God their saviour, which had done great things in
Egypt;<a id="kjv-psalms-106-21"></a><sup>21</sup>

Wondrous works in the land of Ham, and terrible things by the
Red sea.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-22"></a><sup>22</sup>

Therefore he said that he would destroy them, had not Moses his
chosen stood before him in the breach, to turn away his wrath, lest he
should destroy them.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-23"></a><sup>23</sup>

Yea, they despised the pleasant land, they believed not his
word:<a id="kjv-psalms-106-24"></a><sup>24</sup>

But murmured in their tents, and hearkened not unto the voice
of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-25"></a><sup>25</sup>

Therefore he lifted up his hand against them, to overthrow them
in the wilderness:<a id="kjv-psalms-106-26"></a><sup>26</sup>

To overthrow their seed also among the nations, and to scatter
them in the lands.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-27"></a><sup>27</sup>

They joined themselves also unto Baalpeor, and ate the
sacrifices of the dead.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-28"></a><sup>28</sup>

Thus they provoked him to anger with their inventions: and the
plague brake in upon them.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-29"></a><sup>29</sup>

Then stood up Phinehas, and executed judgment: and so the
plague was stayed.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-30"></a><sup>30</sup>

And that was counted unto him for righteousness unto all
generations for evermore.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-31"></a><sup>31</sup>

They angered him also at the waters of strife, so that it went
ill with Moses for their sakes:<a id="kjv-psalms-106-32"></a><sup>32</sup>

Because they provoked his spirit, so that he spake unadvisedly
with his lips.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-33"></a><sup>33</sup>

They did not destroy the nations, concerning whom the LORD
commanded them:<a id="kjv-psalms-106-34"></a><sup>34</sup>

But were mingled among the heathen, and learned their works.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-35"></a><sup>35</sup>

And they served their idols: which were a snare unto them.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-36"></a><sup>36</sup>

Yea, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters unto
devils,<a id="kjv-psalms-106-37"></a><sup>37</sup>

And shed innocent blood, even the blood of their sons and of
their daughters, whom they sacrificed unto the idols of Canaan: and
the land was polluted with blood.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-38"></a><sup>38</sup>

Thus were they defiled with their own works, and went a whoring
with their own inventions.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-39"></a><sup>39</sup>

Therefore was the wrath of the LORD kindled against his people,
insomuch that he abhorred his own inheritance.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-40"></a><sup>40</sup>

And he gave them into the hand of the heathen; and they that
hated them ruled over them.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-41"></a><sup>41</sup>

Their enemies also oppressed them, and they were brought into
subjection under their hand.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-42"></a><sup>42</sup>

Many times did he deliver them; but they provoked him with
their counsel, and were brought low for their iniquity.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-43"></a><sup>43</sup>

Nevertheless he regarded their affliction, when he heard their
cry:<a id="kjv-psalms-106-44"></a><sup>44</sup>

And he remembered for them his covenant, and repented according
to the multitude of his mercies.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-45"></a><sup>45</sup>

He made them also to be pitied of all those that carried them
captives.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-46"></a><sup>46</sup>

Save us, O LORD our God, and gather us from among the heathen,
to give thanks unto thy holy name, and to triumph in thy praise.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-47"></a><sup>47</sup>

Blessed be the LORD God of Israel from everlasting to
everlasting: and let all the people say, Amen. Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-106-48"></a><sup>48</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-107"></a>Chapter 107

O give thanks unto the LORD, for he is good: for his mercy
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Let the redeemed of the LORD say so, whom he hath redeemed from
the hand of the enemy;<a id="kjv-psalms-107-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

And gathered them out of the lands, from the east, and from the
west, from the north, and from the south.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

They wandered in the wilderness in a solitary way; they found no
city to dwell in.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Hungry and thirsty, their soul fainted in them.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Then they cried unto the LORD in their trouble, and he delivered
them out of their distresses.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

And he led them forth by the right way, that they might go to a
city of habitation.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his
wonderful works to the children of men!<a id="kjv-psalms-107-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

For he satisfieth the longing soul, and filleth the hungry soul
with goodness.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Such as sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, being bound
in affliction and iron;<a id="kjv-psalms-107-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Because they rebelled against the words of God, and contemned
the counsel of the most High:<a id="kjv-psalms-107-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

Therefore he brought down their heart with labour; they fell
down, and there was none to help.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

Then they cried unto the LORD in their trouble, and he saved
them out of their distresses.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death, and
brake their bands in sunder.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his
wonderful works to the children of men!<a id="kjv-psalms-107-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

For he hath broken the gates of brass, and cut the bars of iron
in sunder.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

Fools because of their transgression, and because of their
iniquities, are afflicted.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

Their soul abhorreth all manner of meat; and they draw near
unto the gates of death.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

Then they cry unto the LORD in their trouble, and he saveth
them out of their distresses.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

He sent his word, and healed them, and delivered them from
their destructions.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his
wonderful works to the children of men!<a id="kjv-psalms-107-21"></a><sup>21</sup>

And let them sacrifice the sacrifices of thanksgiving, and
declare his works with rejoicing.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-22"></a><sup>22</sup>

They that go down to the sea in ships, that do business in
great waters;<a id="kjv-psalms-107-23"></a><sup>23</sup>

These see the works of the LORD, and his wonders in the deep.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-24"></a><sup>24</sup>

For he commandeth, and raiseth the stormy wind, which lifteth
up the waves thereof.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-25"></a><sup>25</sup>

They mount up to the heaven, they go down again to the depths:
their soul is melted because of trouble.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-26"></a><sup>26</sup>

They reel to and fro, and stagger like a drunken man, and are
at their wit’s end.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-27"></a><sup>27</sup>

Then they cry unto the LORD in their trouble, and he bringeth
them out of their distresses.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-28"></a><sup>28</sup>

He maketh the storm a calm, so that the waves thereof are
still.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-29"></a><sup>29</sup>

Then are they glad because they be quiet; so he bringeth them
unto their desired haven.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-30"></a><sup>30</sup>

Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his
wonderful works to the children of men!<a id="kjv-psalms-107-31"></a><sup>31</sup>

Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the people, and
praise him in the assembly of the elders.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-32"></a><sup>32</sup>

He turneth rivers into a wilderness, and the watersprings into
dry ground;<a id="kjv-psalms-107-33"></a><sup>33</sup>

A fruitful land into barrenness, for the wickedness of them
that dwell therein.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-34"></a><sup>34</sup>

He turneth the wilderness into a standing water, and dry ground
into watersprings.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-35"></a><sup>35</sup>

And there he maketh the hungry to dwell, that they may prepare
a city for habitation;<a id="kjv-psalms-107-36"></a><sup>36</sup>

And sow the fields, and plant vineyards, which may yield fruits
of increase.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-37"></a><sup>37</sup>

He blesseth them also, so that they are multiplied greatly; and
suffereth not their cattle to decrease.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-38"></a><sup>38</sup>

Again, they are minished and brought low through oppression,
affliction, and sorrow.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-39"></a><sup>39</sup>

He poureth contempt upon princes, and causeth them to wander in
the wilderness, where there is no way.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-40"></a><sup>40</sup>

Yet setteth he the poor on high from affliction, and maketh him
families like a flock.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-41"></a><sup>41</sup>

The righteous shall see it, and rejoice: and all iniquity shall
stop her mouth.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-42"></a><sup>42</sup>

Whoso is wise, and will observe these things, even they shall
understand the lovingkindness of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-107-43"></a><sup>43</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-108"></a>Chapter 108

O god, my heart is fixed; I will sing and give praise, even with
my glory.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Awake, psaltery and harp: I myself will awake early.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

I will praise thee, O LORD, among the people: and I will sing
praises unto thee among the nations.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

For thy mercy is great above the heavens: and thy truth reacheth
unto the clouds.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: and thy glory above
all the earth;<a id="kjv-psalms-108-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

That thy beloved may be delivered: save with thy right hand, and
answer me.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide
Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Gilead is mine; Manasseh is mine; Ephraim also is the strength
of mine head; Judah is my lawgiver;<a id="kjv-psalms-108-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Moab is my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe; over
Philistia will I triumph.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into
Edom?<a id="kjv-psalms-108-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us off? and wilt not thou,
O God, go forth with our hosts?<a id="kjv-psalms-108-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

Give us help from trouble: for vain is the help of man.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

Through God we shall do valiantly: for he it is that shall
tread down our enemies.<a id="kjv-psalms-108-13"></a><sup>13</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-109"></a>Chapter 109

Hold not thy peace, O God of my praise;<a id="kjv-psalms-109-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

For the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful are
opened against me: they have spoken against me with a lying tongue.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

They compassed me about also with words of hatred; and fought
against me without a cause.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

For my love they are my adversaries: but I give myself unto
prayer.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

And they have rewarded me evil for good, and hatred for my love.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Set thou a wicked man over him: and let Satan stand at his right
hand.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

When he shall be judged, let him be condemned: and let his
prayer become sin.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Let his days be few; and let another take his office.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Let his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Let his children be continually vagabonds, and beg: let them
seek their bread also out of their desolate places.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Let the extortioner catch all that he hath; and let the
strangers spoil his labour.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

Let there be none to extend mercy unto him: neither let there
be any to favour his fatherless children.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

Let his posterity be cut off; and in the generation following
let their name be blotted out.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with the LORD;
and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

Let them be before the LORD continually, that he may cut off
the memory of them from the earth.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

Because that he remembered not to shew mercy, but persecuted
the poor and needy man, that he might even slay the broken in heart.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

As he loved cursing, so let it come unto him: as he delighted
not in blessing, so let it be far from him.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

As he clothed himself with cursing like as with his garment, so
let it come into his bowels like water, and like oil into his bones.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

Let it be unto him as the garment which covereth him, and for a
girdle wherewith he is girded continually.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

Let this be the reward of mine adversaries from the LORD, and
of them that speak evil against my soul.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

But do thou for me, O GOD the Lord, for thy name’s sake:
because thy mercy is good, deliver thou me.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-21"></a><sup>21</sup>

For I am poor and needy, and my heart is wounded within me.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-22"></a><sup>22</sup>

I am gone like the shadow when it declineth: I am tossed up and
down as the locust.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-23"></a><sup>23</sup>

My knees are weak through fasting; and my flesh faileth of
fatness.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-24"></a><sup>24</sup>

I became also a reproach unto them: when they looked upon me
they shaked their heads.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-25"></a><sup>25</sup>

Help me, O LORD my God: O save me according to thy mercy:<a id="kjv-psalms-109-26"></a><sup>26</sup>

That they may know that this is thy hand; that thou, LORD, hast
done it.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-27"></a><sup>27</sup>

Let them curse, but bless thou: when they arise, let them be
ashamed; but let thy servant rejoice.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-28"></a><sup>28</sup>

Let mine adversaries be clothed with shame, and let them cover
themselves with their own confusion, as with a mantle.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-29"></a><sup>29</sup>

I will greatly praise the LORD with my mouth; yea, I will
praise him among the multitude.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-30"></a><sup>30</sup>

For he shall stand at the right hand of the poor, to save him
from those that condemn his soul.<a id="kjv-psalms-109-31"></a><sup>31</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-110"></a>Chapter 110

The LORD said unto my Lord, Sit thou at my right hand, until I
make thine enemies thy footstool.<a id="kjv-psalms-110-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

The LORD shall send the rod of thy strength out of Zion: rule
thou in the midst of thine enemies.<a id="kjv-psalms-110-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Thy people shall be willing in the day of thy power, in the
beauties of holiness from the womb of the morning: thou hast the dew
of thy youth.<a id="kjv-psalms-110-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

The LORD hath sworn, and will not repent, Thou art a priest for
ever after the order of Melchizedek.<a id="kjv-psalms-110-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

The Lord at thy right hand shall strike through kings in the day
of his wrath.<a id="kjv-psalms-110-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

He shall judge among the heathen, he shall fill the places with
the dead bodies; he shall wound the heads over many countries.<a id="kjv-psalms-110-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

He shall drink of the brook in the way: therefore shall he lift
up the head.<a id="kjv-psalms-110-7"></a><sup>7</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-111"></a>Chapter 111

Praise ye the LORD. I will praise the LORD with my whole heart,
in the assembly of the upright, and in the congregation.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

The works of the LORD are great, sought out of all them that
have pleasure therein.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

His work is honourable and glorious: and his righteousness
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

He hath made his wonderful works to be remembered: the LORD is
gracious and full of compassion.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

He hath given meat unto them that fear him: he will ever be
mindful of his covenant.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

He hath shewed his people the power of his works, that he may
give them the heritage of the heathen.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

The works of his hands are verity and judgment; all his
commandments are sure.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

They stand fast for ever and ever, and are done in truth and
uprightness.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

He sent redemption unto his people: he hath commanded his
covenant for ever: holy and reverend is his name.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom: a good
understanding have all they that do his commandments: his praise
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-111-10"></a><sup>10</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-112"></a>Chapter 112

Praise ye the LORD. Blessed is the man that feareth the LORD,
that delighteth greatly in his commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

His seed shall be mighty upon earth: the generation of the
upright shall be blessed.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Wealth and riches shall be in his house: and his righteousness
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Unto the upright there ariseth light in the darkness: he is
gracious, and full of compassion, and righteous.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

A good man sheweth favour, and lendeth: he will guide his
affairs with discretion.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Surely he shall not be moved for ever: the righteous shall be in
everlasting remembrance.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

He shall not be afraid of evil tidings: his heart is fixed,
trusting in the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

His heart is established, he shall not be afraid, until he see
his desire upon his enemies.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

He hath dispersed, he hath given to the poor; his righteousness
endureth for ever; his horn shall be exalted with honour.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

The wicked shall see it, and be grieved; he shall gnash with
his teeth, and melt away: the desire of the wicked shall perish.<a id="kjv-psalms-112-10"></a><sup>10</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-113"></a>Chapter 113

Praise ye the LORD. Praise, O ye servants of the LORD, praise
the name of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-113-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Blessed be the name of the LORD from this time forth and for
evermore.<a id="kjv-psalms-113-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

From the rising of the sun unto the going down of the same the
LORD’s name is to be praised.<a id="kjv-psalms-113-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

The LORD is high above all nations, and his glory above the
heavens.<a id="kjv-psalms-113-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Who is like unto the LORD our God, who dwelleth on high,<a id="kjv-psalms-113-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Who humbleth himself to behold the things that are in heaven,
and in the earth!<a id="kjv-psalms-113-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

He raiseth up the poor out of the dust, and lifteth the needy
out of the dunghill;<a id="kjv-psalms-113-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

That he may set him with princes, even with the princes of his
people.<a id="kjv-psalms-113-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

He maketh the barren woman to keep house, and to be a joyful
mother of children. Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-113-9"></a><sup>9</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-114"></a>Chapter 114

When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people
of strange language;<a id="kjv-psalms-114-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Judah was his sanctuary, and Israel his dominion.<a id="kjv-psalms-114-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

The sea saw it, and fled: Jordan was driven back.<a id="kjv-psalms-114-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

The mountains skipped like rams, and the little hills like
lambs.<a id="kjv-psalms-114-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

What ailed thee, O thou sea, that thou fleddest? thou Jordan,
that thou wast driven back?<a id="kjv-psalms-114-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Ye mountains, that ye skipped like rams; and ye little hills,
like lambs?<a id="kjv-psalms-114-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Tremble, thou earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the
presence of the God of Jacob;<a id="kjv-psalms-114-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Which turned the rock into a standing water, the flint into a
fountain of waters.<a id="kjv-psalms-114-8"></a><sup>8</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-115"></a>Chapter 115

Not unto us, O LORD, not unto us, but unto thy name give glory,
for thy mercy, and for thy truth’s sake.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Wherefore should the heathen say, Where is now their God?<a id="kjv-psalms-115-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

But our God is in the heavens: he hath done whatsoever he hath
pleased.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Their idols are silver and gold, the work of men’s hands.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

They have mouths, but they speak not: eyes have they, but they
see not:<a id="kjv-psalms-115-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

They have ears, but they hear not: noses have they, but they
smell not:<a id="kjv-psalms-115-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

They have hands, but they handle not: feet have they, but they
walk not: neither speak they through their throat.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

They that make them are like unto them; so is every one that
trusteth in them.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

O Israel, trust thou in the LORD: he is their help and their
shield.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

O house of Aaron, trust in the LORD: he is their help and their
shield.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Ye that fear the LORD, trust in the LORD: he is their help and
their shield.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

The LORD hath been mindful of us: he will bless us; he will
bless the house of Israel; he will bless the house of Aaron.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

He will bless them that fear the LORD, both small and great.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

The LORD shall increase you more and more, you and your
children.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

Ye are blessed of the LORD which made heaven and earth.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

The heaven, even the heavens, are the LORD’s: but the earth
hath he given to the children of men.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

The dead praise not the LORD, neither any that go down into
silence.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

But we will bless the LORD from this time forth and for
evermore.

Praise the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-115-18"></a><sup>18</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-116"></a>Chapter 116

I love the LORD, because he hath heard my voice and my
supplications.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Because he hath inclined his ear unto me, therefore will I call
upon him as long as I live.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

The sorrows of death compassed me, and the pains of hell gat
hold upon me: I found trouble and sorrow.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Then called I upon the name of the LORD; O LORD, I beseech thee,
deliver my soul.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Gracious is the LORD, and righteous; yea, our God is merciful.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

The LORD preserveth the simple: I was brought low, and he helped
me.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Return unto thy rest, O my soul; for the LORD hath dealt
bountifully with thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

For thou hast delivered my soul from death, mine eyes from
tears, and my feet from falling.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

I will walk before the LORD in the land of the living.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

I believed, therefore have I spoken: I was greatly afflicted:<a id="kjv-psalms-116-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

I said in my haste, All men are liars.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

What shall I render unto the LORD for all his benefits toward
me?<a id="kjv-psalms-116-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

I will take the cup of salvation, and call upon the name of the
LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

I will pay my vows unto the LORD now in the presence of all his
people.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

Precious in the sight of the LORD is the death of his saints.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

O LORD, truly I am thy servant; I am thy servant, and the son
of thine handmaid: thou hast loosed my bonds.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

I will offer to thee the sacrifice of thanksgiving, and will
call upon the name of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

I will pay my vows unto the LORD now in the presence of all his
people.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

In the courts of the LORD’s house, in the midst of thee, O
Jerusalem. Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-116-19"></a><sup>19</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-117"></a>Chapter 117

O praise the LORD, all ye nations: praise him, all ye people.<a id="kjv-psalms-117-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

For his merciful kindness is great toward us: and the truth of
the LORD endureth for ever. Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-117-2"></a><sup>2</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-118"></a>Chapter 118

O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: because his mercy
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Let Israel now say, that his mercy endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy endureth for
ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Let them now that fear the LORD say, that his mercy endureth for
ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

I called upon the LORD in distress: the LORD answered me, and
set me in a large place.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

The LORD is on my side; I will not fear: what can man do unto
me?<a id="kjv-psalms-118-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

The LORD taketh my part with them that help me: therefore shall
I see my desire upon them that hate me.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

It is better to trust in the LORD than to put confidence in man.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

It is better to trust in the LORD than to put confidence in
princes.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

All nations compassed me about: but in the name of the LORD
will I destroy them.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

They compassed me about; yea, they compassed me about: but in
the name of the LORD I will destroy them.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

They compassed me about like bees: they are quenched as the
fire of thorns: for in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

Thou hast thrust sore at me that I might fall: but the LORD
helped me.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

The LORD is my strength and song, and is become my salvation.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

The voice of rejoicing and salvation is in the tabernacles of
the righteous: the right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

The right hand of the LORD is exalted: the right hand of the
LORD doeth valiantly.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

I shall not die, but live, and declare the works of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

The LORD hath chastened me sore: but he hath not given me over
unto death.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will go into them, and
I will praise the LORD:<a id="kjv-psalms-118-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

This gate of the LORD, into which the righteous shall enter.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

I will praise thee: for thou hast heard me, and art become my
salvation.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-21"></a><sup>21</sup>

The stone which the builders refused is become the head stone
of the corner.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-22"></a><sup>22</sup>

This is the LORD’s doing; it is marvellous in our eyes.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-23"></a><sup>23</sup>

This is the day which the LORD hath made; we will rejoice and
be glad in it.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-24"></a><sup>24</sup>

Save now, I beseech thee, O LORD: O LORD, I beseech thee, send
now prosperity.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-25"></a><sup>25</sup>

Blessed be he that cometh in the name of the LORD: we have
blessed you out of the house of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-26"></a><sup>26</sup>

God is the LORD, which hath shewed us light: bind the sacrifice
with cords, even unto the horns of the altar.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-27"></a><sup>27</sup>

Thou art my God, and I will praise thee: thou art my God, I
will exalt thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-28"></a><sup>28</sup>

O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-118-29"></a><sup>29</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-119"></a>Chapter 119

Blessed are the undefiled in the way, who walk in the law of the
LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Blessed are they that keep his testimonies, and that seek him
with the whole heart.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

They also do no iniquity: they walk in his ways.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Thou hast commanded us to keep thy precepts diligently.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

O that my ways were directed to keep thy statutes!<a id="kjv-psalms-119-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Then shall I not be ashamed, when I have respect unto all thy
commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, when I shall have
learned thy righteous judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

I will keep thy statutes: O forsake me not utterly.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Wherewithal shall a young man cleanse his way? by taking heed
thereto according to thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

With my whole heart have I sought thee: O let me not wander
from thy commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Thy word have I hid in mine heart, that I might not sin against
thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

Blessed art thou, O LORD: teach me thy statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

With my lips have I declared all the judgments of thy mouth.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

I have rejoiced in the way of thy testimonies, as much as in
all riches.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

I will meditate in thy precepts, and have respect unto thy
ways.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

I will delight myself in thy statutes: I will not forget thy
word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

Deal bountifully with thy servant, that I may live, and keep
thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

Open thou mine eyes, that I may behold wondrous things out of
thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

I am a stranger in the earth: hide not thy commandments from
me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

My soul breaketh for the longing that it hath unto thy
judgments at all times.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

Thou hast rebuked the proud that are cursed, which do err from
thy commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-21"></a><sup>21</sup>

Remove from me reproach and contempt; for I have kept thy
testimonies.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-22"></a><sup>22</sup>

Princes also did sit and speak against me: but thy servant did
meditate in thy statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-23"></a><sup>23</sup>

Thy testimonies also are my delight and my counsellors.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-24"></a><sup>24</sup>

My soul cleaveth unto the dust: quicken thou me according to
thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-25"></a><sup>25</sup>

I have declared my ways, and thou heardest me: teach me thy
statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-26"></a><sup>26</sup>

Make me to understand the way of thy precepts: so shall I talk
of thy wondrous works.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-27"></a><sup>27</sup>

My soul melteth for heaviness: strengthen thou me according
unto thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-28"></a><sup>28</sup>

Remove from me the way of lying: and grant me thy law
graciously.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-29"></a><sup>29</sup>

I have chosen the way of truth: thy judgments have I laid
before me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-30"></a><sup>30</sup>

I have stuck unto thy testimonies: O LORD, put me not to shame.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-31"></a><sup>31</sup>

I will run the way of thy commandments, when thou shalt enlarge
my heart.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-32"></a><sup>32</sup>

Teach me, O LORD, the way of thy statutes; and I shall keep it
unto the end.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-33"></a><sup>33</sup>

Give me understanding, and I shall keep thy law; yea, I shall
observe it with my whole heart.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-34"></a><sup>34</sup>

Make me to go in the path of thy commandments; for therein do I
delight.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-35"></a><sup>35</sup>

Incline my heart unto thy testimonies, and not to covetousness.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-36"></a><sup>36</sup>

Turn away mine eyes from beholding vanity; and quicken thou me
in thy way.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-37"></a><sup>37</sup>

Stablish thy word unto thy servant, who is devoted to thy fear.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-38"></a><sup>38</sup>

Turn away my reproach which I fear: for thy judgments are good.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-39"></a><sup>39</sup>

Behold, I have longed after thy precepts: quicken me in thy
righteousness.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-40"></a><sup>40</sup>

Let thy mercies come also unto me, O LORD, even thy salvation,
according to thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-41"></a><sup>41</sup>

So shall I have wherewith to answer him that reproacheth me:
for I trust in thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-42"></a><sup>42</sup>

And take not the word of truth utterly out of my mouth; for I
have hoped in thy judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-43"></a><sup>43</sup>

So shall I keep thy law continually for ever and ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-44"></a><sup>44</sup>

And I will walk at liberty: for I seek thy precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-45"></a><sup>45</sup>

I will speak of thy testimonies also before kings, and will not
be ashamed.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-46"></a><sup>46</sup>

And I will delight myself in thy commandments, which I have
loved.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-47"></a><sup>47</sup>

My hands also will I lift up unto thy commandments, which I
have loved; and I will meditate in thy statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-48"></a><sup>48</sup>

Remember the word unto thy servant, upon which thou hast caused
me to hope.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-49"></a><sup>49</sup>

This is my comfort in my affliction: for thy word hath
quickened me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-50"></a><sup>50</sup>

The proud have had me greatly in derision: yet have I not
declined from thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-51"></a><sup>51</sup>

I remembered thy judgments of old, O LORD; and have comforted
myself.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-52"></a><sup>52</sup>

Horror hath taken hold upon me because of the wicked that
forsake thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-53"></a><sup>53</sup>

Thy statutes have been my songs in the house of my pilgrimage.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-54"></a><sup>54</sup>

I have remembered thy name, O LORD, in the night, and have kept
thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-55"></a><sup>55</sup>

This I had, because I kept thy precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-56"></a><sup>56</sup>

Thou art my portion, O LORD: I have said that I would keep thy
words.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-57"></a><sup>57</sup>

I intreated thy favour with my whole heart: be merciful unto me
according to thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-58"></a><sup>58</sup>

I thought on my ways, and turned my feet unto thy testimonies.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-59"></a><sup>59</sup>

I made haste, and delayed not to keep thy commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-60"></a><sup>60</sup>

The bands of the wicked have robbed me: but I have not
forgotten thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-61"></a><sup>61</sup>

At midnight I will rise to give thanks unto thee because of thy
righteous judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-62"></a><sup>62</sup>

I am a companion of all them that fear thee, and of them that
keep thy precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-63"></a><sup>63</sup>

The earth, O LORD, is full of thy mercy: teach me thy statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-64"></a><sup>64</sup>

Thou hast dealt well with thy servant, O LORD, according unto
thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-65"></a><sup>65</sup>

Teach me good judgment and knowledge: for I have believed thy
commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-66"></a><sup>66</sup>

Before I was afflicted I went astray: but now have I kept thy
word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-67"></a><sup>67</sup>

Thou art good, and doest good; teach me thy statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-68"></a><sup>68</sup>

The proud have forged a lie against me: but I will keep thy
precepts with my whole heart.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-69"></a><sup>69</sup>

Their heart is as fat as grease; but I delight in thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-70"></a><sup>70</sup>

It is good for me that I have been afflicted; that I might
learn thy statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-71"></a><sup>71</sup>

The law of thy mouth is better unto me than thousands of gold
and silver.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-72"></a><sup>72</sup>

Thy hands have made me and fashioned me: give me understanding,
that I may learn thy commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-73"></a><sup>73</sup>

They that fear thee will be glad when they see me; because I
have hoped in thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-74"></a><sup>74</sup>

I know, O LORD, that thy judgments are right, and that thou in
faithfulness hast afflicted me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-75"></a><sup>75</sup>

Let, I pray thee, thy merciful kindness be for my comfort,
according to thy word unto thy servant.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-76"></a><sup>76</sup>

Let thy tender mercies come unto me, that I may live: for thy
law is my delight.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-77"></a><sup>77</sup>

Let the proud be ashamed; for they dealt perversely with me
without a cause: but I will meditate in thy precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-78"></a><sup>78</sup>

Let those that fear thee turn unto me, and those that have
known thy testimonies.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-79"></a><sup>79</sup>

Let my heart be sound in thy statutes; that I be not ashamed.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-80"></a><sup>80</sup>

My soul fainteth for thy salvation: but I hope in thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-81"></a><sup>81</sup>

Mine eyes fail for thy word, saying, When wilt thou comfort me?<a id="kjv-psalms-119-82"></a><sup>82</sup>

For I am become like a bottle in the smoke; yet do I not forget
thy statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-83"></a><sup>83</sup>

How many are the days of thy servant? when wilt thou execute
judgment on them that persecute me?<a id="kjv-psalms-119-84"></a><sup>84</sup>

The proud have digged pits for me, which are not after thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-85"></a><sup>85</sup>

All thy commandments are faithful: they persecute me
wrongfully; help thou me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-86"></a><sup>86</sup>

They had almost consumed me upon earth; but I forsook not thy
precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-87"></a><sup>87</sup>

Quicken me after thy lovingkindness; so shall I keep the
testimony of thy mouth.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-88"></a><sup>88</sup>

For ever, O LORD, thy word is settled in heaven.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-89"></a><sup>89</sup>

Thy faithfulness is unto all generations: thou hast established
the earth, and it abideth.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-90"></a><sup>90</sup>

They continue this day according to thine ordinances: for all
are thy servants.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-91"></a><sup>91</sup>

Unless thy law had been my delights, I should then have
perished in mine affliction.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-92"></a><sup>92</sup>

I will never forget thy precepts: for with them thou hast
quickened me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-93"></a><sup>93</sup>

I am thine, save me: for I have sought thy precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-94"></a><sup>94</sup>

The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: but I will
consider thy testimonies.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-95"></a><sup>95</sup>

I have seen an end of all perfection: but thy commandment is
exceeding broad.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-96"></a><sup>96</sup>

O how I love thy law! it is my meditation all the day.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-97"></a><sup>97</sup>

Thou through thy commandments hast made me wiser than mine
enemies: for they are ever with me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-98"></a><sup>98</sup>

I have more understanding than all my teachers: for thy
testimonies are my meditation.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-99"></a><sup>99</sup>

I understand more than the ancients, because I keep thy
precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-100"></a><sup>100</sup>

I have refrained my feet from every evil way, that I might
keep thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-101"></a><sup>101</sup>

I have not departed from thy judgments: for thou hast taught
me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-102"></a><sup>102</sup>

How sweet are thy words unto my taste! yea, sweeter than honey
to my mouth!<a id="kjv-psalms-119-103"></a><sup>103</sup>

Through thy precepts I get understanding: therefore I hate
every false way.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-104"></a><sup>104</sup>

Thy word is a lamp unto my feet, and a light unto my path.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-105"></a><sup>105</sup>

I have sworn, and I will perform it, that I will keep thy
righteous judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-106"></a><sup>106</sup>

I am afflicted very much: quicken me, O LORD, according unto
thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-107"></a><sup>107</sup>

Accept, I beseech thee, the freewill offerings of my mouth, O
LORD, and teach me thy judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-108"></a><sup>108</sup>

My soul is continually in my hand: yet do I not forget thy
law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-109"></a><sup>109</sup>

The wicked have laid a snare for me: yet I erred not from thy
precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-110"></a><sup>110</sup>

Thy testimonies have I taken as an heritage for ever: for they
are the rejoicing of my heart.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-111"></a><sup>111</sup>

I have inclined mine heart to perform thy statutes alway, even
unto the end.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-112"></a><sup>112</sup>

I hate vain thoughts: but thy law do I love.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-113"></a><sup>113</sup>

Thou art my hiding place and my shield: I hope in thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-114"></a><sup>114</sup>

Depart from me, ye evildoers: for I will keep the commandments
of my God.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-115"></a><sup>115</sup>

Uphold me according unto thy word, that I may live: and let me
not be ashamed of my hope.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-116"></a><sup>116</sup>

Hold thou me up, and I shall be safe: and I will have respect
unto thy statutes continually.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-117"></a><sup>117</sup>

Thou hast trodden down all them that err from thy statutes:
for their deceit is falsehood.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-118"></a><sup>118</sup>

Thou puttest away all the wicked of the earth like dross:
therefore I love thy testimonies.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-119"></a><sup>119</sup>

My flesh trembleth for fear of thee; and I am afraid of thy
judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-120"></a><sup>120</sup>

I have done judgment and justice: leave me not to mine
oppressors.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-121"></a><sup>121</sup>

Be surety for thy servant for good: let not the proud oppress
me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-122"></a><sup>122</sup>

Mine eyes fail for thy salvation, and for the word of thy
righteousness.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-123"></a><sup>123</sup>

Deal with thy servant according unto thy mercy, and teach me
thy statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-124"></a><sup>124</sup>

I am thy servant; give me understanding, that I may know thy
testimonies.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-125"></a><sup>125</sup>

It is time for thee, LORD, to work: for they have made void
thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-126"></a><sup>126</sup>

Therefore I love thy commandments above gold; yea, above fine
gold.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-127"></a><sup>127</sup>

Therefore I esteem all thy precepts concerning all things to
be right; and I hate every false way.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-128"></a><sup>128</sup>

Thy testimonies are wonderful: therefore doth my soul keep
them.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-129"></a><sup>129</sup>

The entrance of thy words giveth light; it giveth
understanding unto the simple.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-130"></a><sup>130</sup>

I opened my mouth, and panted: for I longed for thy
commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-131"></a><sup>131</sup>

Look thou upon me, and be merciful unto me, as thou usest to
do unto those that love thy name.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-132"></a><sup>132</sup>

Order my steps in thy word: and let not any iniquity have
dominion over me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-133"></a><sup>133</sup>

Deliver me from the oppression of man: so will I keep thy
precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-134"></a><sup>134</sup>

Make thy face to shine upon thy servant; and teach me thy
statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-135"></a><sup>135</sup>

Rivers of waters run down mine eyes, because they keep not thy
law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-136"></a><sup>136</sup>

Righteous art thou, O LORD, and upright are thy judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-137"></a><sup>137</sup>

Thy testimonies that thou hast commanded are righteous and
very faithful.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-138"></a><sup>138</sup>

My zeal hath consumed me, because mine enemies have forgotten
thy words.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-139"></a><sup>139</sup>

Thy word is very pure: therefore thy servant loveth it.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-140"></a><sup>140</sup>

I am small and despised: yet do not I forget thy precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-141"></a><sup>141</sup>

Thy righteousness is an everlasting righteousness, and thy law
is the truth.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-142"></a><sup>142</sup>

Trouble and anguish have taken hold on me: yet thy
commandments are my delights.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-143"></a><sup>143</sup>

The righteousness of thy testimonies is everlasting: give me
understanding, and I shall live.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-144"></a><sup>144</sup>

I cried with my whole heart; hear me, O LORD: I will keep thy
statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-145"></a><sup>145</sup>

I cried unto thee; save me, and I shall keep thy testimonies.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-146"></a><sup>146</sup>

I prevented the dawning of the morning, and cried: I hoped in
thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-147"></a><sup>147</sup>

Mine eyes prevent the night watches, that I might meditate in
thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-148"></a><sup>148</sup>

Hear my voice according unto thy lovingkindness: O LORD,
quicken me according to thy judgment.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-149"></a><sup>149</sup>

They draw nigh that follow after mischief: they are far from
thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-150"></a><sup>150</sup>

Thou art near, O LORD; and all thy commandments are truth.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-151"></a><sup>151</sup>

Concerning thy testimonies, I have known of old that thou hast
founded them for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-152"></a><sup>152</sup>

Consider mine affliction, and deliver me: for I do not forget
thy law.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-153"></a><sup>153</sup>

Plead my cause, and deliver me: quicken me according to thy
word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-154"></a><sup>154</sup>

Salvation is far from the wicked: for they seek not thy
statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-155"></a><sup>155</sup>

Great are thy tender mercies, O LORD: quicken me according to
thy judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-156"></a><sup>156</sup>

Many are my persecutors and mine enemies; yet do I not decline
from thy testimonies.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-157"></a><sup>157</sup>

I beheld the transgressors, and was grieved; because they kept
not thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-158"></a><sup>158</sup>

Consider how I love thy precepts: quicken me, O LORD,
according to thy lovingkindness.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-159"></a><sup>159</sup>

Thy word is true from the beginning: and every one of thy
righteous judgments endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-160"></a><sup>160</sup>

Princes have persecuted me without a cause: but my heart
standeth in awe of thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-161"></a><sup>161</sup>

I rejoice at thy word, as one that findeth great spoil.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-162"></a><sup>162</sup>

I hate and abhor lying: but thy law do I love.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-163"></a><sup>163</sup>

Seven times a day do I praise thee because of thy righteous
judgments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-164"></a><sup>164</sup>

Great peace have they which love thy law: and nothing shall
offend them.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-165"></a><sup>165</sup>

LORD, I have hoped for thy salvation, and done thy
commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-166"></a><sup>166</sup>

My soul hath kept thy testimonies; and I love them
exceedingly.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-167"></a><sup>167</sup>

I have kept thy precepts and thy testimonies: for all my ways
are before thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-168"></a><sup>168</sup>

Let my cry come near before thee, O LORD: give me
understanding according to thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-169"></a><sup>169</sup>

Let my supplication come before thee: deliver me according to
thy word.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-170"></a><sup>170</sup>

My lips shall utter praise, when thou hast taught me thy
statutes.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-171"></a><sup>171</sup>

My tongue shall speak of thy word: for all thy commandments
are righteousness.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-172"></a><sup>172</sup>

Let thine hand help me; for I have chosen thy precepts.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-173"></a><sup>173</sup>

I have longed for thy salvation, O LORD; and thy law is my
delight.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-174"></a><sup>174</sup>

Let my soul live, and it shall praise thee; and let thy
judgments help me.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-175"></a><sup>175</sup>

I have gone astray like a lost sheep; seek thy servant; for I
do not forget thy commandments.<a id="kjv-psalms-119-176"></a><sup>176</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-120"></a>Chapter 120

In my distress I cried unto the LORD, and he heard me.<a id="kjv-psalms-120-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Deliver my soul, O LORD, from lying lips, and from a deceitful
tongue.<a id="kjv-psalms-120-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

What shall be given unto thee? or what shall be done unto thee,
thou false tongue?<a id="kjv-psalms-120-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals of juniper.<a id="kjv-psalms-120-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Woe is me, that I sojourn in Mesech, that I dwell in the tents
of Kedar!<a id="kjv-psalms-120-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

My soul hath long dwelt with him that hateth peace.<a id="kjv-psalms-120-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

I am for peace: but when I speak, they are for war.<a id="kjv-psalms-120-7"></a><sup>7</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-121"></a>Chapter 121

I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my
help.<a id="kjv-psalms-121-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

My help cometh from the LORD, which made heaven and earth.<a id="kjv-psalms-121-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee
will not slumber.<a id="kjv-psalms-121-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep.<a id="kjv-psalms-121-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

The LORD is thy keeper: the LORD is thy shade upon thy right
hand.<a id="kjv-psalms-121-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night.<a id="kjv-psalms-121-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil: he shall preserve
thy soul.<a id="kjv-psalms-121-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in from
this time forth, and even for evermore.<a id="kjv-psalms-121-8"></a><sup>8</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-122"></a>Chapter 122

I was glad when they said unto me, Let us go into the house of
the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-122-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Our feet shall stand within thy gates, O Jerusalem.<a id="kjv-psalms-122-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Jerusalem is builded as a city that is compact together:<a id="kjv-psalms-122-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Whither the tribes go up, the tribes of the LORD, unto the
testimony of Israel, to give thanks unto the name of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-122-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

For there are set thrones of judgment, the thrones of the house
of David.<a id="kjv-psalms-122-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: they shall prosper that love
thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-122-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Peace be within thy walls, and prosperity within thy palaces.<a id="kjv-psalms-122-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

For my brethren and companions’ sakes, I will now say, Peace be
within thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-122-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Because of the house of the LORD our God I will seek thy good.<a id="kjv-psalms-122-9"></a><sup>9</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-123"></a>Chapter 123

Unto thee lift I up mine eyes, O thou that dwellest in the
heavens.<a id="kjv-psalms-123-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Behold, as the eyes of servants look unto the hand of their
masters, and as the eyes of a maiden unto the hand of her mistress; so
our eyes wait upon the LORD our God, until that he have mercy upon us.<a id="kjv-psalms-123-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Have mercy upon us, O LORD, have mercy upon us: for we are
exceedingly filled with contempt.<a id="kjv-psalms-123-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Our soul is exceedingly filled with the scorning of those that
are at ease, and with the contempt of the proud.<a id="kjv-psalms-123-4"></a><sup>4</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-124"></a>Chapter 124

If it had not been the LORD who was on our side, now may Israel
say;<a id="kjv-psalms-124-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

If it had not been the LORD who was on our side, when men rose
up against us:<a id="kjv-psalms-124-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Then they had swallowed us up quick, when their wrath was
kindled against us:<a id="kjv-psalms-124-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Then the waters had overwhelmed us, the stream had gone over our
soul:<a id="kjv-psalms-124-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Then the proud waters had gone over our soul.<a id="kjv-psalms-124-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Blessed be the LORD, who hath not given us as a prey to their
teeth.<a id="kjv-psalms-124-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Our soul is escaped as a bird out of the snare of the fowlers:
the snare is broken, and we are escaped.<a id="kjv-psalms-124-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Our help is in the name of the LORD, who made heaven and earth.<a id="kjv-psalms-124-8"></a><sup>8</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-125"></a>Chapter 125

They that trust in the LORD shall be as mount Zion, which cannot
be removed, but abideth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-125-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

As the mountains are round about Jerusalem, so the LORD is round
about his people from henceforth even for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-125-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

For the rod of the wicked shall not rest upon the lot of the
righteous; lest the righteous put forth their hands unto iniquity.<a id="kjv-psalms-125-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Do good, O LORD, unto those that be good, and to them that are
upright in their hearts.<a id="kjv-psalms-125-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

As for such as turn aside unto their crooked ways, the LORD
shall lead them forth with the workers of iniquity: but peace shall be
upon Israel.<a id="kjv-psalms-125-5"></a><sup>5</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-126"></a>Chapter 126

When the LORD turned again the captivity of Zion, we were like
them that dream.<a id="kjv-psalms-126-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Then was our mouth filled with laughter, and our tongue with
singing: then said they among the heathen, The LORD hath done great
things for them.<a id="kjv-psalms-126-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

The LORD hath done great things for us; whereof we are glad.<a id="kjv-psalms-126-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Turn again our captivity, O LORD, as the streams in the south.<a id="kjv-psalms-126-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

They that sow in tears shall reap in joy.<a id="kjv-psalms-126-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

He that goeth forth and weepeth, bearing precious seed, shall
doubtless come again with rejoicing, bringing his sheaves with him.<a id="kjv-psalms-126-6"></a><sup>6</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-127"></a>Chapter 127

Except the LORD build the house, they labour in vain that build
it: except the LORD keep the city, the watchman waketh but in vain.<a id="kjv-psalms-127-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

It is vain for you to rise up early, to sit up late, to eat the
bread of sorrows: for so he giveth his beloved sleep.<a id="kjv-psalms-127-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Lo, children are an heritage of the LORD: and the fruit of the
womb is his reward.<a id="kjv-psalms-127-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

As arrows are in the hand of a mighty man; so are children of
the youth.<a id="kjv-psalms-127-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Happy is the man that hath his quiver full of them: they shall
not be ashamed, but they shall speak with the enemies in the gate.<a id="kjv-psalms-127-5"></a><sup>5</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-128"></a>Chapter 128

Blessed is every one that feareth the LORD; that walketh in his
ways.<a id="kjv-psalms-128-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

For thou shalt eat the labour of thine hands: happy shalt thou
be, and it shall be well with thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-128-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Thy wife shall be as a fruitful vine by the sides of thine
house: thy children like olive plants round about thy table.<a id="kjv-psalms-128-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Behold, that thus shall the man be blessed that feareth the
LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-128-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

The LORD shall bless thee out of Zion: and thou shalt see the
good of Jerusalem all the days of thy life.<a id="kjv-psalms-128-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Yea, thou shalt see thy children’s children, and peace upon
Israel.<a id="kjv-psalms-128-6"></a><sup>6</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-129"></a>Chapter 129

Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth, may Israel now
say:<a id="kjv-psalms-129-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth: yet they have
not prevailed against me.<a id="kjv-psalms-129-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

The plowers plowed upon my back: they made long their furrows.<a id="kjv-psalms-129-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

The LORD is righteous: he hath cut asunder the cords of the
wicked.<a id="kjv-psalms-129-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Let them all be confounded and turned back that hate Zion.<a id="kjv-psalms-129-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Let them be as the grass upon the housetops, which withereth
afore it groweth up:<a id="kjv-psalms-129-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Wherewith the mower filleth not his hand; nor he that bindeth
sheaves his bosom.<a id="kjv-psalms-129-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Neither do they which go by say, The blessing of the LORD be
upon you: we bless you in the name of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-129-8"></a><sup>8</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-130"></a>Chapter 130

Out of the depths have I cried unto thee, O LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-130-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Lord, hear my voice: let thine ears be attentive to the voice of
my supplications.<a id="kjv-psalms-130-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

If thou, LORD, shouldest mark iniquities, O Lord, who shall
stand?<a id="kjv-psalms-130-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

But there is forgiveness with thee, that thou mayest be feared.<a id="kjv-psalms-130-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

I wait for the LORD, my soul doth wait, and in his word do I
hope.<a id="kjv-psalms-130-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

My soul waiteth for the Lord more than they that watch for the
morning: I say, more than they that watch for the morning.<a id="kjv-psalms-130-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Let Israel hope in the LORD: for with the LORD there is mercy,
and with him is plenteous redemption.<a id="kjv-psalms-130-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

And he shall redeem Israel from all his iniquities.<a id="kjv-psalms-130-8"></a><sup>8</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-131"></a>Chapter 131

Lord, my heart is not haughty, nor mine eyes lofty: neither do I
exercise myself in great matters, or in things too high for me.<a id="kjv-psalms-131-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Surely I have behaved and quieted myself, as a child that is
weaned of his mother: my soul is even as a weaned child.<a id="kjv-psalms-131-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Let Israel hope in the LORD from henceforth and for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-131-3"></a><sup>3</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-132"></a>Chapter 132

Lord, remember David, and all his afflictions:<a id="kjv-psalms-132-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

How he sware unto the LORD, and vowed unto the mighty God of
Jacob;<a id="kjv-psalms-132-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Surely I will not come into the tabernacle of my house, nor go
up into my bed;<a id="kjv-psalms-132-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

I will not give sleep to mine eyes, or slumber to mine eyelids,<a id="kjv-psalms-132-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Until I find out a place for the LORD, an habitation for the
mighty God of Jacob.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Lo, we heard of it at Ephratah: we found it in the fields of the
wood.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

We will go into his tabernacles: we will worship at his
footstool.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Arise, O LORD, into thy rest; thou, and the ark of thy strength.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Let thy priests be clothed with righteousness; and let thy
saints shout for joy.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

For thy servant David’s sake turn not away the face of thine
anointed.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

The LORD hath sworn in truth unto David; he will not turn from
it; Of the fruit of thy body will I set upon thy throne.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

If thy children will keep my covenant and my testimony that I
shall teach them, their children shall also sit upon thy throne for
evermore.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

For the LORD hath chosen Zion; he hath desired it for his
habitation.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

This is my rest for ever: here will I dwell; for I have desired
it.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

I will abundantly bless her provision: I will satisfy her poor
with bread.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

I will also clothe her priests with salvation: and her saints
shall shout aloud for joy.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

There will I make the horn of David to bud: I have ordained a
lamp for mine anointed.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

His enemies will I clothe with shame: but upon himself shall
his crown flourish.<a id="kjv-psalms-132-18"></a><sup>18</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-133"></a>Chapter 133

Behold, how good and how pleasant it is for brethren to dwell
together in unity!<a id="kjv-psalms-133-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

It is like the precious ointment upon the head, that ran down
upon the beard, even Aaron’s beard: that went down to the skirts of
his garments;<a id="kjv-psalms-133-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

As the dew of Hermon, and as the dew that descended upon the
mountains of Zion: for there the LORD commanded the blessing, even
life for evermore.<a id="kjv-psalms-133-3"></a><sup>3</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-134"></a>Chapter 134

Behold, bless ye the LORD, all ye servants of the LORD, which by
night stand in the house of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-134-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Lift up your hands in the sanctuary, and bless the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-134-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

The LORD that made heaven and earth bless thee out of Zion.<a id="kjv-psalms-134-3"></a><sup>3</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-135"></a>Chapter 135

Praise ye the LORD. Praise ye the name of the LORD; praise him,
O ye servants of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Ye that stand in the house of the LORD, in the courts of the
house of our God.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Praise the LORD; for the LORD is good: sing praises unto his
name; for it is pleasant.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

For the LORD hath chosen Jacob unto himself, and Israel for his
peculiar treasure.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

For I know that the LORD is great, and that our Lord is above
all gods.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Whatsoever the LORD pleased, that did he in heaven, and in
earth, in the seas, and all deep places.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

He causeth the vapours to ascend from the ends of the earth; he
maketh lightnings for the rain; he bringeth the wind out of his
treasuries.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Who smote the firstborn of Egypt, both of man and beast.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Who sent tokens and wonders into the midst of thee, O Egypt,
upon Pharaoh, and upon all his servants.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Who smote great nations, and slew mighty kings;<a id="kjv-psalms-135-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Sihon king of the Amorites, and Og king of Bashan, and all the
kingdoms of Canaan:<a id="kjv-psalms-135-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

And gave their land for an heritage, an heritage unto Israel
his people.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

Thy name, O LORD, endureth for ever; and thy memorial, O LORD,
throughout all generations.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

For the LORD will judge his people, and he will repent himself
concerning his servants.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

The idols of the heathen are silver and gold, the work of men’s
hands.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

They have mouths, but they speak not; eyes have they, but they
see not;<a id="kjv-psalms-135-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

They have ears, but they hear not; neither is there any breath
in their mouths.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

They that make them are like unto them: so is every one that
trusteth in them.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

Bless the LORD, O house of Israel: bless the LORD, O house of
Aaron:<a id="kjv-psalms-135-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

Bless the LORD, O house of Levi: ye that fear the LORD, bless
the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

Blessed be the LORD out of Zion, which dwelleth at Jerusalem.

Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-135-21"></a><sup>21</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-136"></a>Chapter 136

O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

O give thanks unto the God of gods: for his mercy endureth for
ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

O give thanks to the Lord of lords: for his mercy endureth for
ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

To him who alone doeth great wonders: for his mercy endureth for
ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

To him that by wisdom made the heavens: for his mercy endureth
for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

To him that stretched out the earth above the waters: for his
mercy endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

To him that made great lights: for his mercy endureth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

The sun to rule by day: for his mercy endureth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

The moon and stars to rule by night: for his mercy endureth for
ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

To him that smote Egypt in their firstborn: for his mercy
endureth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

And brought out Israel from among them: for his mercy endureth
for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

With a strong hand, and with a stretched out arm: for his mercy
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

To him which divided the Red sea into parts: for his mercy
endureth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

And made Israel to pass through the midst of it: for his mercy
endureth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

But overthrew Pharaoh and his host in the Red sea: for his
mercy endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

To him which led his people through the wilderness: for his
mercy endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

To him which smote great kings: for his mercy endureth for
ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

And slew famous kings: for his mercy endureth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

Sihon king of the Amorites: for his mercy endureth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

And Og the king of Bashan: for his mercy endureth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

And gave their land for an heritage: for his mercy endureth for
ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-21"></a><sup>21</sup>

Even an heritage unto Israel his servant: for his mercy
endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-22"></a><sup>22</sup>

Who remembered us in our low estate: for his mercy endureth for
ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-136-23"></a><sup>23</sup>

And hath redeemed us from our enemies: for his mercy endureth
for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-24"></a><sup>24</sup>

Who giveth food to all flesh: for his mercy endureth for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-25"></a><sup>25</sup>

O give thanks unto the God of heaven: for his mercy endureth
for ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-136-26"></a><sup>26</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-137"></a>Chapter 137

By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down, yea, we wept, when
we remembered Zion.<a id="kjv-psalms-137-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

We hanged our harps upon the willows in the midst thereof.<a id="kjv-psalms-137-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

For there they that carried us away captive required of us a
song; and they that wasted us required of us mirth, saying, Sing us
one of the songs of Zion.<a id="kjv-psalms-137-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

How shall we sing the LORD’s song in a strange land?<a id="kjv-psalms-137-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, let my right hand forget her
cunning.<a id="kjv-psalms-137-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

If I do not remember thee, let my tongue cleave to the roof of
my mouth; if I prefer not Jerusalem above my chief joy.<a id="kjv-psalms-137-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Remember, O LORD, the children of Edom in the day of Jerusalem;
who said, Rase it, rase it, even to the foundation thereof.<a id="kjv-psalms-137-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

O daughter of Babylon, who art to be destroyed; happy shall he
be, that rewardeth thee as thou hast served us.<a id="kjv-psalms-137-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Happy shall he be, that taketh and dasheth thy little ones
against the stones.<a id="kjv-psalms-137-9"></a><sup>9</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-138"></a>Chapter 138

I will praise thee with my whole heart: before the gods will I
sing praise unto thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-138-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

I will worship toward thy holy temple, and praise thy name for
thy lovingkindness and for thy truth: for thou hast magnified thy word
above all thy name.<a id="kjv-psalms-138-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

In the day when I cried thou answeredst me, and strengthenedst
me with strength in my soul.<a id="kjv-psalms-138-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

All the kings of the earth shall praise thee, O LORD, when they
hear the words of thy mouth.<a id="kjv-psalms-138-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Yea, they shall sing in the ways of the LORD: for great is the
glory of the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-138-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Though the LORD be high, yet hath he respect unto the lowly: but
the proud he knoweth afar off.<a id="kjv-psalms-138-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Though I walk in the midst of trouble, thou wilt revive me: thou
shalt stretch forth thine hand against the wrath of mine enemies, and
thy right hand shall save me.<a id="kjv-psalms-138-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

The LORD will perfect that which concerneth me: thy mercy, O
LORD, endureth for ever: forsake not the works of thine own hands.<a id="kjv-psalms-138-8"></a><sup>8</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-139"></a>Chapter 139

O lord, thou hast searched me, and known me.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Thou knowest my downsitting and mine uprising, thou
understandest my thought afar off.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Thou compassest my path and my lying down, and art acquainted
with all my ways.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

For there is not a word in my tongue, but, lo, O LORD, thou
knowest it altogether.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Thou hast beset me behind and before, and laid thine hand upon
me.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Such knowledge is too wonderful for me; it is high, I cannot
attain unto it.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or whither shall I flee from
thy presence?<a id="kjv-psalms-139-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

If I ascend up into heaven, thou art there: if I make my bed in
hell, behold, thou art there.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

If I take the wings of the morning, and dwell in the uttermost
parts of the sea;<a id="kjv-psalms-139-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Even there shall thy hand lead me, and thy right hand shall
hold me.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

If I say, Surely the darkness shall cover me; even the night
shall be light about me.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

Yea, the darkness hideth not from thee; but the night shineth
as the day: the darkness and the light are both alike to thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

For thou hast possessed my reins: thou hast covered me in my
mother’s womb.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

I will praise thee; for I am fearfully and wonderfully made:
marvellous are thy works; and that my soul knoweth right well.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

My substance was not hid from thee, when I was made in secret,
and curiously wrought in the lowest parts of the earth.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

Thine eyes did see my substance, yet being unperfect; and in
thy book all my members were written, which in continuance were
fashioned, when as yet there was none of them.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

How precious also are thy thoughts unto me, O God! how great is
the sum of them!<a id="kjv-psalms-139-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

If I should count them, they are more in number than the sand:
when I awake, I am still with thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

Surely thou wilt slay the wicked, O God: depart from me
therefore, ye bloody men.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

For they speak against thee wickedly, and thine enemies take
thy name in vain.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

Do not I hate them, O LORD, that hate thee? and am not I
grieved with those that rise up against thee?<a id="kjv-psalms-139-21"></a><sup>21</sup>

I hate them with perfect hatred: I count them mine enemies.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-22"></a><sup>22</sup>

Search me, O God, and know my heart: try me, and know my
thoughts:<a id="kjv-psalms-139-23"></a><sup>23</sup>

And see if there be any wicked way in me, and lead me in the
way everlasting.<a id="kjv-psalms-139-24"></a><sup>24</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-140"></a>Chapter 140

Deliver me, O LORD, from the evil man: preserve me from the
violent man;<a id="kjv-psalms-140-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Which imagine mischiefs in their heart; continually are they
gathered together for war.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent; adders’ poison
is under their lips. Selah.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Keep me, O LORD, from the hands of the wicked; preserve me from
the violent man; who have purposed to overthrow my goings.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

The proud have hid a snare for me, and cords; they have spread a
net by the wayside; they have set gins for me. Selah.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

I said unto the LORD, Thou art my God: hear the voice of my
supplications, O LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

O GOD the Lord, the strength of my salvation, thou hast covered
my head in the day of battle.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Grant not, O LORD, the desires of the wicked: further not his
wicked device; lest they exalt themselves. Selah.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

As for the head of those that compass me about, let the mischief
of their own lips cover them.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Let burning coals fall upon them: let them be cast into the
fire; into deep pits, that they rise not up again.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Let not an evil speaker be established in the earth: evil shall
hunt the violent man to overthrow him.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

I know that the LORD will maintain the cause of the afflicted,
and the right of the poor.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

Surely the righteous shall give thanks unto thy name: the
upright shall dwell in thy presence.<a id="kjv-psalms-140-13"></a><sup>13</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-141"></a>Chapter 141

Lord, I cry unto thee: make haste unto me; give ear unto my
voice, when I cry unto thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Let my prayer be set forth before thee as incense; and the
lifting up of my hands as the evening sacrifice.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Set a watch, O LORD, before my mouth; keep the door of my lips.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Incline not my heart to any evil thing, to practise wicked works
with men that work iniquity: and let me not eat of their dainties.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Let the righteous smite me; it shall be a kindness: and let him
reprove me; it shall be an excellent oil, which shall not break my
head: for yet my prayer also shall be in their calamities.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

When their judges are overthrown in stony places, they shall
hear my words; for they are sweet.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Our bones are scattered at the grave’s mouth, as when one
cutteth and cleaveth wood upon the earth.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

But mine eyes are unto thee, O GOD the Lord: in thee is my
trust; leave not my soul destitute.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Keep me from the snares which they have laid for me, and the
gins of the workers of iniquity.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Let the wicked fall into their own nets, whilst that I withal
escape.<a id="kjv-psalms-141-10"></a><sup>10</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-142"></a>Chapter 142

I cried unto the LORD with my voice; with my voice unto the LORD
did I make my supplication.<a id="kjv-psalms-142-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

I poured out my complaint before him; I shewed before him my
trouble.<a id="kjv-psalms-142-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, then thou knewest my
path.

In the way wherein I walked have they privily laid a snare for me.<a id="kjv-psalms-142-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

I looked on my right hand, and beheld, but there was no man that
would know me: refuge failed me; no man cared for my soul.<a id="kjv-psalms-142-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

I cried unto thee, O LORD: I said, Thou art my refuge and my
portion in the land of the living.<a id="kjv-psalms-142-5"></a><sup>5</sup>
