Attend unto my cry; for I am brought very low: deliver me from
my persecutors; for they are stronger than I.<a id="kjv-psalms-142-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Bring my soul out of prison, that I may praise thy name: the
righteous shall compass me about; for thou shalt deal bountifully with
me.<a id="kjv-psalms-142-7"></a><sup>7</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-143"></a>Chapter 143

Hear my prayer, O LORD, give ear to my supplications: in thy
faithfulness answer me, and in thy righteousness.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

And enter not into judgment with thy servant: for in thy sight
shall no man living be justified.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

For the enemy hath persecuted my soul; he hath smitten my life
down to the ground; he hath made me to dwell in darkness, as those
that have been long dead.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Therefore is my spirit overwhelmed within me; my heart within me
is desolate.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

I remember the days of old; I meditate on all thy works; I muse
on the work of thy hands.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

I stretch forth my hands unto thee: my soul thirsteth after
thee, as a thirsty land. Selah.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Hear me speedily, O LORD: my spirit faileth: hide not thy face
from me, lest I be like unto them that go down into the pit.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Cause me to hear thy lovingkindness in the morning; for in thee
do I trust: cause me to know the way wherein I should walk; for I lift
up my soul unto thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Deliver me, O LORD, from mine enemies: I flee unto thee to hide
me.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Teach me to do thy will; for thou art my God: thy spirit is
good; lead me into the land of uprightness.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Quicken me, O LORD, for thy name’s sake: for thy righteousness’
sake bring my soul out of trouble.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

And of thy mercy cut off mine enemies, and destroy all them
that afflict my soul: for I am thy servant.<a id="kjv-psalms-143-12"></a><sup>12</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-144"></a>Chapter 144

Blessed be the LORD my strength, which teacheth my hands to war,
and my fingers to fight:<a id="kjv-psalms-144-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

My goodness, and my fortress; my high tower, and my deliverer;
my shield, and he in whom I trust; who subdueth my people under me.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

LORD, what is man, that thou takest knowledge of him! or the son
of man, that thou makest account of him!<a id="kjv-psalms-144-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Man is like to vanity: his days are as a shadow that passeth
away.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Bow thy heavens, O LORD, and come down: touch the mountains, and
they shall smoke.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Cast forth lightning, and scatter them: shoot out thine arrows,
and destroy them.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Send thine hand from above; rid me, and deliver me out of great
waters, from the hand of strange children;<a id="kjv-psalms-144-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right
hand of falsehood.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

I will sing a new song unto thee, O God: upon a psaltery and an
instrument of ten strings will I sing praises unto thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

It is he that giveth salvation unto kings: who delivereth David
his servant from the hurtful sword.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Rid me, and deliver me from the hand of strange children, whose
mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of
falsehood:<a id="kjv-psalms-144-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

That our sons may be as plants grown up in their youth; that
our daughters may be as corner stones, polished after the similitude
of a palace:<a id="kjv-psalms-144-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

That our garners may be full, affording all manner of store:
that our sheep may bring forth thousands and ten thousands in our
streets:<a id="kjv-psalms-144-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

That our oxen may be strong to labour; that there be no
breaking in, nor going out; that there be no complaining in our
streets.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

Happy is that people, that is in such a case: yea, happy is
that people, whose God is the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-144-15"></a><sup>15</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-145"></a>Chapter 145

I will extol thee, my God, O king; and I will bless thy name for
ever and ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Every day will I bless thee; and I will praise thy name for ever
and ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised; and his greatness
is unsearchable.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

One generation shall praise thy works to another, and shall
declare thy mighty acts.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

I will speak of the glorious honour of thy majesty, and of thy
wondrous works.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

And men shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and I
will declare thy greatness.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great goodness,
and shall sing of thy righteousness.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

The LORD is gracious, and full of compassion; slow to anger, and
of great mercy.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

The LORD is good to all: and his tender mercies are over all his
works.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

All thy works shall praise thee, O LORD; and thy saints shall
bless thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom, and talk of thy
power;<a id="kjv-psalms-145-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, and the
glorious majesty of his kingdom.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

Thy kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and thy dominion
endureth throughout all generations.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

The LORD upholdeth all that fall, and raiseth up all those that
be bowed down.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

The eyes of all wait upon thee; and thou givest them their meat
in due season.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

Thou openest thine hand, and satisfiest the desire of every
living thing.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

The LORD is righteous in all his ways, and holy in all his
works.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

The LORD is nigh unto all them that call upon him, to all that
call upon him in truth.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

He will fulfil the desire of them that fear him: he also will
hear their cry, and will save them.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

The LORD preserveth all them that love him: but all the wicked
will he destroy.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-20"></a><sup>20</sup>

My mouth shall speak the praise of the LORD: and let all flesh
bless his holy name for ever and ever.<a id="kjv-psalms-145-21"></a><sup>21</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-146"></a>Chapter 146

Praise ye the LORD. Praise the LORD, O my soul.<a id="kjv-psalms-146-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

While I live will I praise the LORD: I will sing praises unto my
God while I have any being.<a id="kjv-psalms-146-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Put not your trust in princes, nor in the son of man, in whom
there is no help.<a id="kjv-psalms-146-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; in that very
day his thoughts perish.<a id="kjv-psalms-146-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Happy is he that hath the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope
is in the LORD his God:<a id="kjv-psalms-146-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Which made heaven, and earth, the sea, and all that therein is:
which keepeth truth for ever:<a id="kjv-psalms-146-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Which executeth judgment for the oppressed: which giveth food to
the hungry. The LORD looseth the prisoners:<a id="kjv-psalms-146-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

The LORD openeth the eyes of the blind: the LORD raiseth them
that are bowed down: the LORD loveth the righteous:<a id="kjv-psalms-146-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

The LORD preserveth the strangers; he relieveth the fatherless
and widow: but the way of the wicked he turneth upside down.<a id="kjv-psalms-146-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

The LORD shall reign for ever, even thy God, O Zion, unto all
generations. Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-146-10"></a><sup>10</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-147"></a>Chapter 147

Praise ye the LORD: for it is good to sing praises unto our God;
for it is pleasant; and praise is comely.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

The LORD doth build up Jerusalem: he gathereth together the
outcasts of Israel.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

He healeth the broken in heart, and bindeth up their wounds.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

He telleth the number of the stars; he calleth them all by their
names.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Great is our Lord, and of great power: his understanding is
infinite.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

The LORD lifteth up the meek: he casteth the wicked down to the
ground.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Sing unto the LORD with thanksgiving; sing praise upon the harp
unto our God:<a id="kjv-psalms-147-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Who covereth the heaven with clouds, who prepareth rain for the
earth, who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

He giveth to the beast his food, and to the young ravens which
cry.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

He delighteth not in the strength of the horse: he taketh not
pleasure in the legs of a man.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

The LORD taketh pleasure in them that fear him, in those that
hope in his mercy.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

Praise the LORD, O Jerusalem; praise thy God, O Zion.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; he hath blessed
thy children within thee.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

He maketh peace in thy borders, and filleth thee with the
finest of the wheat.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-14"></a><sup>14</sup>

He sendeth forth his commandment upon earth: his word runneth
very swiftly.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-15"></a><sup>15</sup>

He giveth snow like wool: he scattereth the hoarfrost like
ashes.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-16"></a><sup>16</sup>

He casteth forth his ice like morsels: who can stand before his
cold?<a id="kjv-psalms-147-17"></a><sup>17</sup>

He sendeth out his word, and melteth them: he causeth his wind
to blow, and the waters flow.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-18"></a><sup>18</sup>

He sheweth his word unto Jacob, his statutes and his judgments
unto Israel.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-19"></a><sup>19</sup>

He hath not dealt so with any nation: and as for his judgments,
they have not known them. Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-147-20"></a><sup>20</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-148"></a>Chapter 148

Praise ye the LORD. Praise ye the LORD from the heavens: praise
him in the heights.<a id="kjv-psalms-148-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Praise ye him, all his angels: praise ye him, all his hosts.<a id="kjv-psalms-148-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Praise ye him, sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars of light.<a id="kjv-psalms-148-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, and ye waters that be above
the heavens.<a id="kjv-psalms-148-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Let them praise the name of the LORD: for he commanded, and they
were created.<a id="kjv-psalms-148-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

He hath also stablished them for ever and ever: he hath made a
decree which shall not pass.<a id="kjv-psalms-148-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

Praise the LORD from the earth, ye dragons, and all deeps:<a id="kjv-psalms-148-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

Fire, and hail; snow, and vapours; stormy wind fulfilling his
word:<a id="kjv-psalms-148-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

Mountains, and all hills; fruitful trees, and all cedars:<a id="kjv-psalms-148-9"></a><sup>9</sup>

Beasts, and all cattle; creeping things, and flying fowl:<a id="kjv-psalms-148-10"></a><sup>10</sup>

Kings of the earth, and all people; princes, and all judges of
the earth:<a id="kjv-psalms-148-11"></a><sup>11</sup>

Both young men, and maidens; old men, and children:<a id="kjv-psalms-148-12"></a><sup>12</sup>

Let them praise the name of the LORD: for his name alone is
excellent; his glory is above the earth and heaven.<a id="kjv-psalms-148-13"></a><sup>13</sup>

He also exalteth the horn of his people, the praise of all his
saints; even of the children of Israel, a people near unto him. Praise
ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-148-14"></a><sup>14</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-149"></a>Chapter 149

Praise ye the LORD. Sing unto the LORD a new song, and his
praise in the congregation of saints.<a id="kjv-psalms-149-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: let the children of
Zion be joyful in their King.<a id="kjv-psalms-149-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Let them praise his name in the dance: let them sing praises
unto him with the timbrel and harp.<a id="kjv-psalms-149-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

For the LORD taketh pleasure in his people: he will beautify the
meek with salvation.<a id="kjv-psalms-149-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Let the saints be joyful in glory: let them sing aloud upon
their beds.<a id="kjv-psalms-149-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Let the high praises of God be in their mouth, and a two-edged
sword in their hand;<a id="kjv-psalms-149-6"></a><sup>6</sup>

To execute vengeance upon the heathen, and punishments upon the
people;<a id="kjv-psalms-149-7"></a><sup>7</sup>

To bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with fetters
of iron;<a id="kjv-psalms-149-8"></a><sup>8</sup>

To execute upon them the judgment written: this honour have all
his saints. Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-149-9"></a><sup>9</sup>


### <a id="kjv-psalms-150"></a>Chapter 150

Praise ye the LORD. Praise God in his sanctuary: praise him in
the firmament of his power.<a id="kjv-psalms-150-1"></a><sup>1</sup>

Praise him for his mighty acts: praise him according to his
excellent greatness.<a id="kjv-psalms-150-2"></a><sup>2</sup>

Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: praise him with the
psaltery and harp.<a id="kjv-psalms-150-3"></a><sup>3</sup>

Praise him with the timbrel and dance: praise him with stringed
instruments and organs.<a id="kjv-psalms-150-4"></a><sup>4</sup>

Praise him upon the loud cymbals: praise him upon the high
sounding cymbals.<a id="kjv-psalms-150-5"></a><sup>5</sup>

Let every thing that hath breath praise the LORD. Praise ye the LORD.<a id="kjv-psalms-150-6"></a><sup>6</sup>
